      <script type="text/javascript">
       function getStatsForThemeMiniStats() {
		// Call ajax request only if data is not here.
		if ($("#upv_416336").text() == "Loading..." ) {
			jQuery.getJSON("/stats/theme/416336?view=json", function(json){
				jQuery("#upv_416336").empty();
				if (json.stats &amp;&amp; json.stats.uniqueVisitors &gt;= 0) {
					jQuery("#upv_416336").append(json.stats.uniqueVisitors);				
				} else {
					jQuery("#upv_416336").append("Not available");
				}
			});
		}
	}
      </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var themeActionsBanner = null;
	jQuery(document).ready(function() {
		themeActionsBanner = jQuery("#theme-actions-banner");
		jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
			if(parseInt(jQuery(this).scrollTop(), 10) &gt; 51) {
				themeActionsBanner.addClass("theme-actions-banner-fixed");
				jQuery("#admin-stuff").css("top", "41px");
			} else {
				themeActionsBanner.removeClass("theme-actions-banner-fixed");
				jQuery("#admin-stuff").css("top", "10px");
			}
		});
	});
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    var logoContainer;
		var infosContainer;
		var logoToHome;
		jQuery(document).ready(function() {
			logoContainer = jQuery(".headSection.head-section-logo");
			infosContainer = jQuery(".headSection.head-section-infos");

			logoToHome = jQuery("#logoToHome", logoContainer);
			//makes the logo Rumble
			logoToHome.jrumble({
				x: 0,
				y: 0,
				rotation: 4,
				speed: 75
			});
			logoToHome.hover(function() {
				var logo = $(this);
				logo.trigger('startRumble');
				// Stop 500ms after
				setTimeout(function() {
					logo.trigger('stopRumble');
				}, 500);
			}, function(){
				$(this).trigger('stopRumble');
			});
		});
   </script>

              <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
               <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4029190257" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 The iconic clock from Grand Central Terminal symbolizes the heart of New York City in this impressive 90-second animated film from Y&amp;R, part of its campaign in backing the New York Organ Donor Network.
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 With the rates of organ donation lower in New York compared to other parts of the United States, a short video has been made with the help of an Oscar winning director to help raise awareness on organ donation.
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Tor read more on the story click on the banner headline. To view the video click on the following link-
                </p>
                <p>
                 <a href="http://youtu.be/uX4MXwNjQQw" rel="nofollow">
                  http://youtu.be/uX4MXwNjQQw
                 </a>
                </p>

                   <p>
                    The latest campaign in the United States is the ECHO Social Media Campaign to Increase Awareness of Organ Donation.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This well thought through campaign aims to create awareness of the importance of organ donation across all sectors of the community.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4046647097">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.swissinfo.ch/eng/money-saver_the-economics-of-organ-donation/41509850" onclick="trackPostClick(4046647097 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   The economics of organ donation - via swissinfo.ch
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.swissinfo.ch/eng/money-saver_the-economics-of-organ-donation/41509850" onclick="trackPostClick(4046647097); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="The economics of organ donation - via swissinfo.ch | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="310" id="postImage_4046647097" src="http://img.scoop.it/humAb_oyU-sHhOif3XiMRzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 310;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.swissinfo.ch/eng/money-saver_the-economics-of-organ-donation/41509850" onclick="trackPostClick(4046647097); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .swissinfo
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .ch
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4046647097/2015/06/28/the-economics-of-organ-donation-via-swissinfo-ch">
                    June 27, 9:59 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046647097">
                   <p>
                    Organ donation not only saves lives, it makes economic sense. That is the latest argument from the organisation promoting organ donation in Switzerland. This forms part of an ongoing strategy to educate the public about the importance of organ donation.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Included in the article is a video which outlines the cost differential between a patient who undergoes a successful kidney transplant versus one who remains on dialysis for a number of years
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://medicor.nu/waiting-in-line/" onclick="trackPostClick(4045841089 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Waiting in Line for an organ transplant in Sweden
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://medicor.nu/waiting-in-line/" onclick="trackPostClick(4045841089); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Waiting in Line for an organ transplant in Sweden | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="310" id="postImage_4045841089" src="http://img.scoop.it/reD71_cgwHB9P-wAyhqOvTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 310;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://medicor.nu/waiting-in-line/" onclick="trackPostClick(4045841089); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   medicor
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .nu
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4045841089/2015/06/16/waiting-in-line-for-an-organ-transplant-in-sweden">
                    June 16, 4:01 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4045841089">
                   <p>
                    The Issue of Organ Donation in Sweden and How to Tackle it is told by Oskar Swartling, with Photos by Martin Kjellberg and Helena Wahlman  
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    It features the stories of two individuals who each have had to join a waiting list before they could be transplanted and hence are able to provide their unique insights into the process from a patients' perspective. "It is very hard to describe the waiting, Martha Ehlin (pictured) says. Peter Carstedt talks about his experience of having to cope with his own kidneys failing, followed by then waiting for a kidney transplant.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    For the full story click on the banner headline
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>

                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   A unique insight into the organ donation and transplant systems in Sweden from two young people who have required organ transplantation in order to restore each of them to relatively good health.
                  </p>
                 </div>

                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://focusnews.com/photos/photo-essay-transplant-surgeons-save-childrens-lives-in-venezuela/48999/" onclick="trackPostClick(4045287212 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Photo Essay: Miracle In Venezuela facilitated by a US Transplant Surgeon and a local healthcare team
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://focusnews.com/photos/photo-essay-transplant-surgeons-save-childrens-lives-in-venezuela/48999/" onclick="trackPostClick(4045287212); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Photo Essay: Miracle In Venezuela facilitated by a US Transplant Surgeon and a local healthcare team | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="313" id="postImage_4045287212" src="http://img.scoop.it/e_lDZa9_Ka7z2QZmRgTdKTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 313;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://focusnews.com/photos/photo-essay-transplant-surgeons-save-childrens-lives-in-venezuela/48999/" onclick="trackPostClick(4045287212); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   focusnews
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4045287212/2015/06/08/photo-essay-miracle-in-venezuela-facilitated-by-a-us-transplant-surgeon-and-a-local-healthcare-team">
                    June 7, 8:10 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4045287212">
                   <p>
                    From Venezuela comes this pictorial essay of how a US-based transplant surgeon came to perform organ transplants on children living in this South American country where a number of medical resources are scarce.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Follow the story of Dr Tomoaki Kato from the United States, who with the assistance of a local team of healthcare professionals has been able to undertake. a number of live donor kidney and liver transplants on children. To date over 50 children have received transplants.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>

                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PTt1P-4vnt0" onclick="trackPostClick(4044202017 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   A man and his dog : innovative, moving advertising with an important message
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-htmlfragment htmlfragment">
                  <object height="253" width="450">
                   <param name="movie" value="https://www.youtube.com/v/PTt1P-4vnt0?fs=1&amp;hl=fr_FR">

                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PTt1P-4vnt0" onclick="trackPostClick(4044202017); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .youtube
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>

                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4044202017/2015/05/23/a-man-and-his-dog-innovative-moving-advertising-with-an-important-message">

                   </a>
                  </span>

                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4044202017">
                   <p>
                    A video has emerged from a moving advertising campaign in Argentina which is being used to deliver a very important message.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This is about the enduring love of a dog and its master, an older man. The man spends the day with his faithful companion. Both are very attentive to each other and are used to being in each others company. Then tragedy strikes......
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Either click on the video image, access the video via the header to this post or click on the following link to watch-
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <a href="https://youtu.be/xYkMV1mf9fU" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                     https://youtu.be/xYkMV1mf9fU
                    </a>
                   </p>

              <div data-lid="4043539481" data-tlid="416336" data-viewmode="" id="post_4043539481">
               <div class="post-from postFrom">

                 <div class="rescoop">

                   <img src="/resources/img/post/icon_rescoop.png"/>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4043539481">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.post-gazette.com/local/region/2015/05/12/Journal-article-suggests-wider-push-for-organ-donation/stories/201505120069" onclick="trackPostClick(4043539481 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Journal article suggests wider push for organ donation within the United States
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.post-gazette.com/local/region/2015/05/12/Journal-article-suggests-wider-push-for-organ-donation/stories/201505120069" onclick="trackPostClick(4043539481); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Journal article suggests wider push for organ donation within the United States | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="311" id="postImage_4043539481" src="http://img.scoop.it/iDM1gNMQQBw49vVy-8AUwTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 311;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.post-gazette.com/local/region/2015/05/12/Journal-article-suggests-wider-push-for-organ-donation/stories/201505120069" onclick="trackPostClick(4043539481); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .post-gazette
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4043539481/2015/05/14/journal-article-suggests-wider-push-for-organ-donation-within-the-united-states">
                    May 13, 1:49 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4043539481">
                   <p>
                    The U.S. health care system could significantly cut waiting times for transplants if there were established processes to recover organs from people who die outside of hospitals or in the emergency department.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This is the theme of an article published online this last week by The
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Journal of the American Medical Association (JAMA). In that article the authors argue that more organs could be retrieved if so called Uncontrolled Donation After Circulatory Death organ donation (UCDCD), was able to occur. This article is published online and is available to view via open access-
                    <a href="http://jama.jamanetwork.com/article.aspx?articleid=2293309" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                     http://jama.jamanetwork.com/article.aspx?articleid=2293309
                    </a>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    However there remain significant barriers to the establishment of UCDCD in many regions in the United States, some of which are mentioned in this post which can be accessed via clicking on the above banner headline. Of note mention is made of the poor results of one pilot study of UCDCD performed in a large city within the US.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   In theory UCDCD appears an attractive pathway via which more organs can be retrieved for the purposes of transplantation. However there remain significant barriers to establishing this practice in many countries. The barriers include meeting legislative and regulatory requirements, establishing and implementing the requisite protocols, healthcare organization and community acceptance and finally cost.
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4042553088">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/health/article-3051430/Britain-s-youngest-organ-donor-Parents-tell-heartbreaking-decision-donate-kidneys-heart-valves-hero-twin-son-Teddy-lived-100-minutes.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4042553088 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Parent's of Teddy Houlston, Britain's youngest ever organ donor Teddy, tell all
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/health/article-3051430/Britain-s-youngest-organ-donor-Parents-tell-heartbreaking-decision-donate-kidneys-heart-valves-hero-twin-son-Teddy-lived-100-minutes.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4042553088); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Parent's of Teddy Houlston, Britain's youngest ever organ donor Teddy, tell all | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="475" id="postImage_4042553088" src="http://img.scoop.it/Hjk4kWDr4EC09ACZlRhS0zl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 475;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/health/article-3051430/Britain-s-youngest-organ-donor-Parents-tell-heartbreaking-decision-donate-kidneys-heart-valves-hero-twin-son-Teddy-lived-100-minutes.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4042553088); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .dailymail
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .co
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .uk
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4042553088/2015/04/30/parent-s-of-teddy-houlston-britain-s-youngest-ever-organ-donor-teddy-tell-all">
                    April 30, 2:59 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4042553088">
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Jess Evans, 28, and her fiance Mike Houlston, 30, from Cardiff, Wales, described their son Teddy as a 'hero' after deciding to donate his organs when he died just 100 minutes after being born.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Teddy was born with anencephaly, whilst his twin brother was completely healthy. What then happened is well described in this online article which can be viewed by clicking on the above banner headline. A short YouTube video can be viewed via this link-
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <a href="https://youtu.be/9UWb3lsQQ_g" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                     https://youtu.be/9UWb3lsQQ_g
                    </a>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    The full video of the interview with Jess and Mike can be viewed via this link-
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <a href="https://youtu.be/VgrjFtquXc8" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                     https://youtu.be/VgrjFtquXc8
                    </a>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    The publicity which followed the release of this story has led to an increase in registrations on the organ donor registry in the United Kingdom-
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <a href="http://www.bbc.com/news/uk-wales-south-east-wales-32510335" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                     http://www.bbc.com/news/uk-wales-south-east-wales-32510335
                    </a>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   An extraordinary story which has also generated a lot of attention via social media including the #Teddysstory thread on Twitter.
                  </p>

              <div data-lid="4041511488" data-tlid="416336" data-viewmode="" id="post_4041511488">
               <div class="post-from postFrom">
                <table class="post-history posthistory">
                 <tr>

                   <a class=" preview-profile" href="http://www.scoop.it/u/deborah-verran">

               <div class="post-view postView post-embed left big ">

                 <div class="rescoop">
                  <div class="button button-rescoop default " onclick="showSignupPopup(null, null, '?rescoop=4041511488');return false;" x-data-rescoop-onclick="showPostInScoopitWindow('/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4041511488/2015/04/16/should-patients-be-able-to-find-organ-donors-on-facebook/rescoop/2', null)">
                   <img src="/resources/img/post/icon_rescoop.png"/>
                   <span>
                    Scoop.it!
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4041511488">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.theatlantic.com/health/archive/2015/04/should-patients-be-able-to-find-organ-donors-on-facebook/390144/" onclick="trackPostClick(4041511488 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Should Patients Be Able to Find Organ Donors on Facebook?
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.theatlantic.com/health/archive/2015/04/should-patients-be-able-to-find-organ-donors-on-facebook/390144/" onclick="trackPostClick(4041511488); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Should Patients Be Able to Find Organ Donors on Facebook? | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="289" id="postImage_4041511488" src="http://img.scoop.it/QOAe1MMkk4k3k11tFqeAkzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 289;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.theatlantic.com/health/archive/2015/04/should-patients-be-able-to-find-organ-donors-on-facebook/390144/" onclick="trackPostClick(4041511488); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .theatlantic
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4041511488/2015/04/16/should-patients-be-able-to-find-organ-donors-on-facebook">
                    April 16, 3:16 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4041511488">
                   <p>
                    A recent case in Belgium, in which a man took to social media to ask for a kidney, is raising questions within the healthcare community in that country about who can ethically donate. In this particular case no final decision has been made.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This article explores the differences currently seen between some of the countries around the world as to whether a 'Facebook' friend would be considered a legitimate friend who would then be eligible to be a kidney donor to a patient with chronic kidney disease.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    It also explores the underutilized organ donation option that is also available via Facebook in a number of countries around the world. To read more on this story click on the banner headline.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   In an era where Facebook has become a vital social networking tool for many people in the community it is legitimate to ask whether friendships established via Facebook meet the same criteria as conventional friendships when the offer to donate an organ is made.
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://matangitonga.to/2015/03/18/ikale-tahi-flanker-praying-kidney-transplant" onclick="trackPostClick(4039617267 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Tongan rugby flanker praying for a kidney transplant
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://matangitonga.to/2015/03/18/ikale-tahi-flanker-praying-kidney-transplant" onclick="trackPostClick(4039617267); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Tongan rugby flanker praying for a kidney transplant | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="259" id="postImage_4039617267" src="http://img.scoop.it/RVwsRuhS_D6e2BpGirFGADl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 259;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://matangitonga.to/2015/03/18/ikale-tahi-flanker-praying-kidney-transplant" onclick="trackPostClick(4039617267); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   matangitonga
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .to
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4039617267/2015/03/21/tongan-rugby-flanker-praying-for-a-kidney-transplant">

                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4039617267">
                   <p>
                    Sione Vaiomounga, who is a rugby football flanker and a Tongan rugby export to Romania, is now suffering from a life threatening kidney disease and requires a kidneytransplant.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Despite now being on dialysis three times a week whilst in Romania, Sione now faces an uphill battle in order to be able to undergo a kidney transplant due to his status as a Tongan national.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    More on the story can be accessed by clicking on the banner headline.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>

                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   This story highlights the problems faced by individuals who are citizens of countries where there are currently limited options for renal replacement therapies.
                  </p>
                 </div>

                   <img src="/resources/img/post/icon_rescoop.png"/>

                    Scoop.it!
                   </span>

                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4038366692">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.thedailybeast.com/articles/2015/02/28/a-head-transplant-is-a-terrible-horrible-no-good-very-bad-idea.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4038366692 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Opinion: Head Transplants are a Possibility - and are a Terrible Idea.
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.thedailybeast.com/articles/2015/02/28/a-head-transplant-is-a-terrible-horrible-no-good-very-bad-idea.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4038366692); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Opinion: Head Transplants are a Possibility - and are a Terrible Idea. | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="292" id="postImage_4038366692" src="http://img.scoop.it/4ZeQHdxIwgEZg8Wc3j86DDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 292;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.thedailybeast.com/articles/2015/02/28/a-head-transplant-is-a-terrible-horrible-no-good-very-bad-idea.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4038366692); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .thedailybeast
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4038366692/2015/03/03/opinion-head-transplants-are-a-possibility-and-are-a-terrible-idea">
                    March 3, 2:09 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4038366692">
                   <p>
                    Recently it has been widely reported that an Italian doctor now claims that head transplants could be possibly performed in the next two years.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    However as stated in this online opinion the big question now is "But just because we can, does that mean we should'?
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    There are major concerns about the outcome of such a procedure noting that most of the body of an organ donor would be required to replace the old body of the recipient. This leads to significant issues around whether the transplant procedure will truly lead to the outcome that is intended. There will be issues with maintaining a whole new body on ant-rejection agents whilst it is hoped that the spinal cord in particular could heal enough for full function of the arms and legs to be restored.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    The easy to read article can be accessed by clicking on the banner headline.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   Currently one organ donor can provide organs and tissue that benefit the lives of a number of people. To then use one organ donor for an experimental procedure with an unknown outcome raises many questions.
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                   <img src="/resources/img/post/icon_rescoop.png"/>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4036821505">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.dailytelegraph.com.au/news/nsw/rare-transplant-dead-heart-used-to-give-sydney-man-a-new-lease-on-life/story-fni0cx12-1227211695670?nk=85a0617a14cdd3eb964f4fdd9cfafef5" onclick="trackPostClick(4036821505 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Rare transplant: Heart from a DCD donor used to give Sydney man a new lease on life
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.dailytelegraph.com.au/news/nsw/rare-transplant-dead-heart-used-to-give-sydney-man-a-new-lease-on-life/story-fni0cx12-1227211695670?nk=85a0617a14cdd3eb964f4fdd9cfafef5" onclick="trackPostClick(4036821505); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Rare transplant: Heart from a DCD donor used to give Sydney man a new lease on life | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="350" id="postImage_4036821505" src="http://img.scoop.it/3TvMRF_wHbLkBds6CThJtTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 350;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.dailytelegraph.com.au/news/nsw/rare-transplant-dead-heart-used-to-give-sydney-man-a-new-lease-on-life/story-fni0cx12-1227211695670?nk=85a0617a14cdd3eb964f4fdd9cfafef5" onclick="trackPostClick(4036821505); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .dailytelegraph
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .au
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4036821505/2015/02/08/rare-transplant-heart-from-a-dcd-donor-used-to-give-sydney-man-a-new-lease-on-life">
                    February 7, 7:31 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4036821505">
                   <p>
                    TONY Sakr was on his way to Christmas Eve dinner with his family when he finally got the one gift he had been waiting for a new donor heart.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    What was different in this case was that the heart would be retrieved from an organ donor who had been declared dead following cessation of their own circulation.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This would mean that the donor's heart had ceased beating prior to the organ retrieval surgery commencing. In order to check on the viability of the donor heart following its removal from the donor, an ex-vivo organ preservation machine was used (pictured lower right hand corner of the image).
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    The donor heart was placed onto this machine and watched for a period of time prior to its then successful transplantation into Mr Sakr. Video footage of the donor heart functioning prior to transplantation is able to be viewed by clicking on the banner headline to this story.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   The report of another case of successful heart transplantation from a DCD (Donation after circulatory Death) organ donor in Australia
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.ctvnews.ca/health/ont-sets-new-record-for-organ-donation-helping-save-more-than-1-000-lives-1.2211639" onclick="trackPostClick(4036308837 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Ontario sets new record for organ donation in 2014, helping save more than 1000 lives
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.ctvnews.ca/health/ont-sets-new-record-for-organ-donation-helping-save-more-than-1-000-lives-1.2211639" onclick="trackPostClick(4036308837); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

                    News from Ontario, Canada that a new record for organ donations was set in 2014 that helped save more than 1,000 lives. This news was released via the agency for organ, tissue and transplant, Trillium Gift of Life.

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4035227376">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.rediff.com/news/report/indias-first-ever-hand-transplant-successfully-conducted-in-kerala/20150114.htm" onclick="trackPostClick(4035227376 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   India's first-ever hand transplant successfully conducted in Kerala
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.rediff.com/news/report/indias-first-ever-hand-transplant-successfully-conducted-in-kerala/20150114.htm" onclick="trackPostClick(4035227376); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="India's first-ever hand transplant successfully conducted in Kerala | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="307" id="postImage_4035227376" src="http://img.scoop.it/vhkJE6hSiP2VTjDfhwyBWDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 307;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.rediff.com/news/report/indias-first-ever-hand-transplant-successfully-conducted-in-kerala/20150114.htm" onclick="trackPostClick(4035227376); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .rediff
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4035227376/2015/01/14/india-s-first-ever-hand-transplant-successfully-conducted-in-kerala">
                    January 14, 1:51 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4035227376">
                   <p>
                    In a marathon 16-hour-long surgery, doctors at the Kochi-based Amrita Institute of Medical Sciences and Research Centre successfully conducted India's first hand transplant this last week.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    The bilateral hand transplant was performed on a young man who had previously lost both of his hands in an accident. The hands were donated by a young organ donor.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    As this is a preliminary report there is no other details at this stage
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">

                 </div>

                  <p>
                   Important news from India of what is an uncommonly performed transplant procedure
                  </p>
                 </div>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4047202929">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://nocamels.com/2011/07/an-israeli-storybook-garden-is-all-heart" onclick="trackPostClick(4047202929 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Holons Storybook Gardens Teach Children About Organ Donation
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://nocamels.com/2011/07/an-israeli-storybook-garden-is-all-heart" onclick="trackPostClick(4047202929); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Holons Storybook Gardens Teach Children About Organ Donation | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="314" id="postImage_4047202929" src="http://img.scoop.it/osMZAd74qSPX7xWdH1OlGTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 314;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://nocamels.com/2011/07/an-israeli-storybook-garden-is-all-heart" onclick="trackPostClick(4047202929); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   nocamels
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4047202929/2015/07/07/holon-s-storybook-gardens-teach-children-about-organ-donation">
                    July 7, 3:56 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047202929">
                   <p>
                    Walking through Israel's city Holon is a little like walking into a fairytale: In recent years the city has turned many of its gardens into live storybooks, with giant statues based on characters from famous children's books.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This particular garden teaches children about heart transplantation based on a character in a storybook. More information on this story can be viewed by clicking on the banner headline.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.walesonline.co.uk/news/wales-news/watch-dancers-blue-morph-suits-9365502" onclick="trackPostClick(4044930131 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Watch blue Morph suit dancers greet commuters at Cardiff Central station
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.walesonline.co.uk/news/wales-news/watch-dancers-blue-morph-suits-9365502" onclick="trackPostClick(4044930131); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Watch blue Morph suit dancers greet commuters at Cardiff Central station | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="311" id="postImage_4044930131" src="http://img.scoop.it/v628XEOwI2rKPC5Mb49lnzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 311;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.walesonline.co.uk/news/wales-news/watch-dancers-blue-morph-suits-9365502" onclick="trackPostClick(4044930131); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .walesonline
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .co
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .uk
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4044930131/2015/06/02/watch-blue-morph-suit-dancers-greet-commuters-at-cardiff-central-station">
                    June 2, 3:31 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4044930131">
                   <p>
                    Crowds of commuters gathered to watch the dancers in blue suits strutting their stuff to the Bee Gees hit Stayin' Alive near Cardiff Central train station recently.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This event is part of an ongoing campaign in Wales to promote conversations around organ donation in light of the looming switch to a soft opt out system for organ donation later this year.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    More information on this story as well as access to a short video of the dancers can be accessed by clicking on the banner headline to thisstory
                   </p>
                  </div>

                  </p>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.reveal.co.uk/real-life-stories/news/a647595/im-climbing-a-19000ft-mountain-to-say-thank-you-after-a-double-lung-transplant.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4043755618 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   "I'm climbing a 19000ft mountain to say thank you after a double lung transplant" - Reveal
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.reveal.co.uk/real-life-stories/news/a647595/im-climbing-a-19000ft-mountain-to-say-thank-you-after-a-double-lung-transplant.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4043755618); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="&quot;I'm climbing a 19000ft mountain to say thank you after a double lung transplant&quot; - Reveal | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="469" id="postImage_4043755618" src="http://img.scoop.it/Bo0d0Q05guKpa1vbITVhsTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 469;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.reveal.co.uk/real-life-stories/news/a647595/im-climbing-a-19000ft-mountain-to-say-thank-you-after-a-double-lung-transplant.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4043755618); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

                    May 16, 11:17 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4043755618">
                   <p>
                    Amanda Chalmers, 27, from Brighton, United Kingdom is part of the "Climbing for my Donor" team which hopes to scale a 19,000 foot mountain in the middle of this year.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Amanda (pictured) has previously undergone a life saving double lung transplant procedure and is undertaking this climb to help raise awareness about organ donation.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>

                   Many transplant recipients continue to advocate for organ donation awareness following their recovery. This is just one example.
                  </p>

                   <img src="/resources/img/post/icon_rescoop.png"/>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4043197581">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://magazine.good.is/articles/brazilian-ice-sculptures-encourage-organ-donation" onclick="trackPostClick(4043197581 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Brazilian Ice Sculptures Encourage Organ Donation via Innovative Concept and Design
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://magazine.good.is/articles/brazilian-ice-sculptures-encourage-organ-donation" onclick="trackPostClick(4043197581); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Brazilian Ice Sculptures Encourage Organ Donation via Innovative Concept and Design | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="312" id="postImage_4043197581" src="http://img.scoop.it/p4Kp_1IQfG8LwnmaohfFpjl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 312;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://magazine.good.is/articles/brazilian-ice-sculptures-encourage-organ-donation" onclick="trackPostClick(4043197581); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   magazine
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .good
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .is
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4043197581/2015/05/09/brazilian-ice-sculptures-encourage-organ-donation-via-innovative-concept-and-design">
                    May 9, 3:27 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4043197581">
                   <p>
                    This report comes from So Paulo, Brazil where a new public art campaign is aimed at getting the local residents to consider organ donation.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This involves the creation of ice statues that are then placed around the city. As the ice melts a solid organ becomes increasingly visible inside the statue. This is to serve as a reminder that the organs from an organ donor can continue to survive once transplanted into another person.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   An innovative way of getting the message about organ donation through to the general public
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                   <p>
                    Will a new app attract more young people to become organ donors? Its developers in Switzerland now hope that this will be the case.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This short video outlines how the app works as well as the information which can be accessed. The video can also be viewed by clicking on the banner headline.

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4040167370">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://metronews.ca/news/vancouver/1325189/kidneys-from-older-patients-may-help-seniors-on-transplant-wait-list-b-c-study/" onclick="trackPostClick(4040167370 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Kidneys from older donors may help seniors on transplant wait list: North American research
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://metronews.ca/news/vancouver/1325189/kidneys-from-older-patients-may-help-seniors-on-transplant-wait-list-b-c-study/" onclick="trackPostClick(4040167370); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Kidneys from older donors may help seniors on transplant wait list: North American research | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="309" id="postImage_4040167370" src="http://img.scoop.it/hE7h5cJ53diNiTKx68nAhDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 309;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://metronews.ca/news/vancouver/1325189/kidneys-from-older-patients-may-help-seniors-on-transplant-wait-list-b-c-study/" onclick="trackPostClick(4040167370); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   metronews
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .ca
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4040167370/2015/03/29/kidneys-from-older-donors-may-help-seniors-on-transplant-wait-list-north-american-research">
                    March 28, 9:28 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4040167370">
                   <p>
                    Older patients in need of a kidney transplant are better off receiving organs from older deceased donors than waiting for one from a younger donor, suggests new research from the University of B.C.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    This is the conclusion of researchers who have analysed data from both NorthAmerica and Europe. This research has been published online by the Journal of the American Society of Nephrology.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    A more detailed report can be accessed via the following link-
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <a href="http://www.eurekalert.org/pub_releases/2015-03/ason-wtd031915.php" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                     http://www.eurekalert.org/pub_releases/2015-03/ason-wtd031915.php
                    </a>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   With the high discard rates of kidneys from donors aged over 60 years, particularly in the United States, attention is now turning to how best to utilize these organs.
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4038838249">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2984489/The-organ-snatchers-Boy-12-smuggled-UK-gang-sell-body-parts-black-market.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4038838249 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   12 year old smuggled into UK for gang to sell his body parts on black market
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2984489/The-organ-snatchers-Boy-12-smuggled-UK-gang-sell-body-parts-black-market.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4038838249); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="12 year old smuggled into UK for gang to sell his body parts on black market | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="311" id="postImage_4038838249" src="http://img.scoop.it/oBoy3PMl4SIQ3svbjWVzUzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 311;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2984489/The-organ-snatchers-Boy-12-smuggled-UK-gang-sell-body-parts-black-market.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4038838249); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .dailymail
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .co
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .uk
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4038838249/2015/03/10/12-year-old-smuggled-into-uk-for-gang-to-sell-his-body-parts-on-black-market">
                    March 10, 1:54 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4038838249">
                   <p>
                    Authorities in the United Kingdom have recently released information that two people - a boy between 12 and 15 and a woman in her 30s - have been rescued by police, who suspected that they were being trafficked for the purposes of organ donation.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    The United Kingdom has robust processes in place to prevent organ trafficking from occurring. However internationally organ trafficking remains an issue and the article contains some information on one of the cases for which the perpetrators was recently successfully prosecuted in Europe.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Deborah Verran's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   This story also highlights the lengths that organ traffickers are prepared to go to to obtain organs often from poorly educated disadvantaged individuals. It makes for disturbing reading.
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4037445035">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://women.asiaone.com/women/relationships/hubby-gives-wife-kidney-nuhs-most-challenging-kidney-transplant" onclick="trackPostClick(4037445035 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Husband donates a kidney to his wife in Singapore
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://women.asiaone.com/women/relationships/hubby-gives-wife-kidney-nuhs-most-challenging-kidney-transplant" onclick="trackPostClick(4037445035); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Husband donates a kidney to his wife in Singapore | Organ Donation &amp; Transplant Matters | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="305" id="postImage_4037445035" src="http://img.scoop.it/8NSWhGkHBt7aDQCxtNqwiDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 305;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://women.asiaone.com/women/relationships/hubby-gives-wife-kidney-nuhs-most-challenging-kidney-transplant" onclick="trackPostClick(4037445035); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   women
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .asiaone
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/organ-donation-transplant-matters/p/4037445035/2015/02/17/husband-donates-a-kidney-to-his-wife-in-singapore">
                    February 17, 12:57 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4037445035">
                   <p>
                    Meet the couple behind NUH's most challenging kidney transplant last year (pictured). Security supervisor Mohamad Rafae Asral, 40, admits he is not a romantic man. He is not given to marking Valentine's Day with gifts or special meals for his wife. However after watching Puspawati trying to withstand the rigours of dialysis Mohamed decided to step in and offered to donate one of his kidneys.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    The surgery was carried out last year and to date it has been successful. For more on the story click on the banner headline.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

									                        		                        			                            &lt;p&gt;A six day old baby recently became the youngest organ donor to date in the United Kingdom. The girl&rsquo;s parents have been praised for their courage in allowing the donation and were said to be happy something positive had come from her death&lt;/p&gt;
		                        		                        		                        		    	                    		                        	                        	                        
					    &lt;/div&gt;

				    						    	&lt;/div&gt;
				    	&lt;div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description"&gt;
				    			&lt;p&gt;Although not common it is possible on occasion for small babies to be organ donors if they meet strict medical eligibility criteria&lt;/p&gt;

         <script type="text/javascript">
          jQuery(document).ready(function() {
  			var siteGuid = 'f3ee344206df0c6d0ae2ac138cf16fc8';
  			var userId = $.cookie("grvinsights");
  			if (userId == null) {
  				userId = "unknown";
  			}
  			var current_url = window.location.href;
  			var limit = 3;
  			var url = 'http://rma-api.gravity.com/v0/site/' + siteGuid + '/user/' + userId + '/stories?current_url=' + encodeURI(current_url) + '&amp;limit=' + parseInt(limit, 10) +"&amp;rec_type=sponsored" + '&amp;c=?';
  			$.ajax({
  			    type: 'GET',
  			    dataType: 'jsonp',
  			    url: url,
  			    success: function (data) {
  			    	if (data.status.httpCode == 200){
  			    		var payload = data.payload;
					var ads = jQuery(".gravity");
					jQuery(payload).each(function (index, article) {
						var adpost = jQuery(jQuery(ads).get(index));
						if (typeof(adpost) != "undefined") {
							// title
							jQuery("h2 a", adpost).attr("href", article.url).text(article.title);
							// image
							var image = jQuery(".post-image", adpost);
							jQuery("a", image).attr("href", article.url);
							jQuery("img", image).data("original", article.image).lazyload({
						    	failure_limit: 20
						    });
							// description
							jQuery(".post-description blockquote", adpost).text(article.summary);
							// domain
							
							var url = document.createElement('a');
							url.href = article.targetUrl;
							jQuery(".post-metas a", adpost).text(url.hostname).attr("href", article.url);
							// show
							adpost.show();
							
							// Is there a post to print?
							var gravityItems = jQuery("#gravity-items");
							if (gravityItems.length &gt; 0) {
								var gravityItem = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-item' /&gt;");
								
								// Image
								var gravityImage = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-image' /&gt;");
								gravityImage.css({
									backgroundImage: "url('"+article.image+"')"
								});
								gravityItem.append(gravityImage);
								gravityImage.wrap("&lt;a href='"+ article.url+"'  target='_blank' rel='nofollow' /&gt;");
								
								// Title
								var gravityTitle = jQuery("&lt;h3 &gt;"+article.title+"&lt;/h3&gt;");
								gravityItem.append(gravityTitle);
								gravityTitle.wrapInner("&lt;a href='"+ article.url+"' target='_blank' rel='nofollow'/&gt;");
								
								// Source
								var gravitySource = jQuery("&lt;div class='gravity-source'&gt;From &lt;/div&gt;");
								var gravitySourceA = jQuery("&lt;a /&gt;");
								gravitySourceA.attr("href", article.url);
								gravitySourceA.text(url.hostname);
								gravitySourceA.attr("target", "_blank");
								gravitySourceA.attr("rel", "nofollow");
								
								gravitySource.append(gravitySourceA);
								gravityItem.append(gravitySource);
								
								// Track click
								jQuery("a", gravityItem).each(function() {
									jQuery(this).click(function() {
										trackClick("clickOnGravityAds", function() {return true;}, null);
									});
								});
								
								gravityItems.append(gravityItem);
							}
						}
					});
					jQuery("#gravity-items").fadeIn();
  			    	} else {
  			    	}
  			       
  			    },
  			    error: function (e) {
  			    }
  			});
  		});
         </script>

	twttr.events.bind('tweet', function(event) {

	});

function linkedinShareSuccess(e) {
	var location = jQuery(".linkedin-share-button[data-href='"+e+"']").attr("data-location");
	var url = e;
	trackNativeButtonShare('linkedin', location, url);
}

(function() {
    var po = document.createElement('script'); po.type = 'text/javascript'; po.async = true;
    po.src = 'https://apis.google.com/js/plusone.js';

function googlePlusTouched(e) {
	if (e.state == "on") {
		var url = e.href;
		var location = "bottomOfPost";
		trackNativeButtonShare('google', location, url);
	}
}


function loadSocialWidgetInAPost(post) {
	if (post.length &gt; 0) {
		//facebook
		if (typeof FB != 'undefined') {
			FB.XFBML.parse(jQuery(".share-button-fb",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-fb");
		}
		//twitter
		if (typeof twttr != 'undefined') {
			jQuery(".share-button-tw a", post).addClass("twitter-share-button");
			twttr.widgets.load(jQuery(".share-button-tw",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-tw");
		}
		//G+
		if (typeof gapi != 'undefined') {
			gapi.plusone.go(jQuery(".share-button-gp",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-gp");
		}
	}
}


function loadVisibleSharers() {
	jQuery(".post").each(function(){
		var elt = jQuery(this);
		if (elt.attr("id") == "topic-tags-widget") {
			return;
		}
		if (elt.hasClass("loaded-tw") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-gp") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-fb")) {return;}
		if (elt.isOnScreen()) {
			loadSocialWidgetInAPost(elt);
		}
	});
}

jQuery(window).bind("resize", function(event) {
	loadVisibleSharers();
});

var scrollingChecker = 0;
function onScroll(event) {
	clearTimeout(scrollingChecker);
	scrollingChecker = setTimeout(onStopScrolling, 300);
}

function onStopScrolling() {
	loadVisibleSharers();
}

jQuery(document).bind("scroll", onScroll);
